  <meta content="Hello everyone my name is DJ Quincy Ortiz am a young talented Chillout DJ and Producer from Maryland, USA. I started DJing in 1998 at the age of 10. My first gig was at a local house party and I was playing House music and Rap at the time. After my first gig I continue to play locally then I decided to try to DJ in clubs in Washington, D.C. My first club I DJ at was Fur night club. It was a wonderful experience but I soon got bored of playing mainstream music. In 2007 I got the chance to travel to Europe and that is when I was introduced to Chill out Music. After that I play chill out music even now.

I made this sexy chill out mix for the radio podcast competition and it falls into the Music mix category. When I was selecting the tracks for the mix most of the songs have the them of Goodbye Yellowbrick Road. The reason why is because all my songs in my mix talk about the feelings of love and harmony. Just like the song Goodbye Yellowbrick Road. Well I hope you like my chill out mix." property="og:description"/>

          <div class="cloudcast-description">
           <p>
            Hello everyone my name is DJ Quincy Ortiz am a young talented Chillout DJ and Producer from Maryland, USA. I started DJing in 1998 at the age of 10. My first gig was at a local house party and I was playing House music and Rap at the time. After my first gig I continue to play locally then I decided to try to DJ in clubs in Washington, D.C. My first club I DJ at was Fur night club. It was a wonderful experience but I soon got bored of playing mainstream music. In 2007 I got the chance to travel to Europe and that is when I was introduced to Chill out Music. After that I play chill out music even now.
           </p>
           <p>
            I made this sexy chill out mix for the radio podcast competition and it falls into the Music mix category. When I was selecting the tracks for the mix most of the songs have the them of Goodbye Yellowbrick Road. The reason why is because all my songs in my mix talk about the feelings of love and harmony. Just like the song Goodbye Yellowbrick Road. Well I hope you like my chill out mix.
           </p>
          </div>
